[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` cannot be launched inside the Docker container. The shell[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing session.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What the issue is  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During an OSS-Fuzz style invocation, a harness script sets up environment [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariables [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFUZZER, TESTCASE, RUN_FUZZER_MODE, FUZZING_ENGINE, SKIP_SEED_CORPUS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls the `run_fuzzer` helper with `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`, memory limits, timeouts, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe test case path. The helper then tries to execute `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`, but [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe shell immediately errors out with:  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    bash: [0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m: Permission denied  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    subprocess command returned a non-zero exit status: [0m[1;36m126[0m[39m  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  No software vulnerability in the `dav1d` code under test is exposed; this is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpurely a permission/configuration issue preventing the binary from executing.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‚Ä¢ The fuzzer binary is mounted into the container at `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` from the host build [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‚Ä¢ The container is run with `--privileged` and ample shared memory, yet execution[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis blocked by file permission bits.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‚Ä¢ Exit code [0m[1;36m126[0m[39m indicates the file exists but is not marked executable in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontainer‚Äôs context.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‚Ä¢ The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`run_fuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m does not modify file permissions‚Äîit assumes the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbinary is already executable.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Codebase areas to investigate  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Build scripts and Makefiles [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor CMake rules[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that produce `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder `build/out/`, to ensure they set the execute bit.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Deployment or copy steps that place the binary into the `out` directory‚Äîverify[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthey preserve file mode.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The OSS-Fuzz `run_fuzzer` wrapper and Docker invocation parameters in the [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpermissions.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Identify and confirm the root cause**  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The fuzzer executables [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are built by Meson[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut never marked with `install: true`. Under OSS-Fuzz‚Äôs flow, only installed [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargets end up under `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` with correct file modes. Since these two fuzzers aren‚Äôt[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstalled, the container sees them without execute permissions, triggering [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m‚ÄúPermission denied.‚Äù[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Patch the Meson build definitions**  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`, locate the two `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` invocations [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` and add the install directive. For each [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget, extend the argument list by inserting:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ‚Ä¢ `install: true`  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Optionally, you can also specify `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to be [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicit about installing into the standard binary directory, but `install: true` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malone is sufficient to pick up `bindir` by default.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Specifically:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35merror[0m[1;39m([0m[39m [0m[32m'C symbol XXH3_createState not found in header xxhash.h'[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m51[0m[39m:    endif[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m52:e[0m[39mndif[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m54:da[0m[39mv1d_input_objs = [0m[1;35mstatic_library[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_input'[0m[39m,[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[39m:    dav1d_input_sources,[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:    include_directories : dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:    install : false,[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:    build_by_default : false,[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default : false,[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35msubdir_done[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m74:e[0m[39mndif[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m51:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m69[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:51[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m59[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m51:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m69[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzing executables `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` are defined in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`, but lack any `install:` directive. Meson does not [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstall these binaries into the build prefix‚Äôs `bindir`, so when OSS-Fuzz runs [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`meson install` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith `-[0m[33mDprefix[0m[39m=$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the fuzzer binaries never get copied into [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`$OUT/bin` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich is mounted to `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and thus remain non-installed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-executable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the build tree. This leads to the ‚ÄúPermission denied‚Äù [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen the harness tries to run `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must leave existing fuzzer source lists, include directories, linker flags,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand build-by-default stanzas intact so that Meson still builds the fuzzers.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter any harness or test code, nor remove any functionality [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mbitdepth loops, assembly options, thread dependencies, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Strategy[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. In `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`, locate the definitions of `dav1d_fuzzer` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m51[0m[39m‚Äì[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m61[0m[39m‚Äì[0m[1;36m69[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. For each `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call, add two keyword arguments:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‚Ä¢ `install: true`  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‚Ä¢ `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This ensures that on `ninja install` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtriggered by OSS-Fuzz[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, Meson will copy [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboth binaries into the installation `bindir` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mby default `$prefix/bin`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserve executable permissions.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Do not modify any other files [0m[1;39m([0m[39mespecially harness or external library code[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Re-run the OSS-Fuzz build:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‚Ä¢ Meson configuration will pick up the new `install:` stanzas.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‚Ä¢ `ninja install` will emit `[0m[35m/out/bin/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m` and [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/bin/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` with `-rwxr-xr-x` modes.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‚Ä¢ The harness will now successfully execute `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This patch directly addresses the missing installation step that prevented the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbinaries from being placed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand marked executable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It mirrors the pattern in `tools/meson.build`, where the main `dav1d` binary [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muses `install: true, install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It does not touch cached Meson files [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`~[0m[35m/.cache/[0m[95m...[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m‚Äîinstead, it applies [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanly to the project‚Äôs own `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, fuzzing engine, or test code is modified, preserving existing test[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuites and fuzz workflows.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Installing additional executables has negligible risk; Meson will simply write[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe two fuzzers into the bindir alongside other tools.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If OSS-Fuzz changes its default `bindir` location, Meson‚Äôs [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` will adapt automatically, keeping the installation path in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msync.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No conflicts with other install targets are expected, since the fuzzer names [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare unique.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Post-Patch Validation[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that `ls -l [0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` shows `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` with [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable bits.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rerun the OSS-Fuzz reproduction command; verify that the fuzzer launches [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than exiting [0m[1;36m126[0m[39m.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing test suites to ensure no regressions.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m51:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:objcopy = [0m[1;35mfind_program[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'objcopy'[0m[39m,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:                       required: false[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mobjcopy.found[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:    not [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'b_lto'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'default_library'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[32m'static'[0m[39m and[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mcc.has_function[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'posix_memalign'[0m[39m, prefix : [0m[32m'#include <stdlib.h>'[0m[39m, args : [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest_args[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Analysis of the OSS-Fuzz build logs and the Meson project layout shows that the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwo fuzzing executables [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdav1d_fuzzer and dav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are being built but [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnever installed into the `$OUT` directory used by the OSS-Fuzz runner. Because [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMeson‚Äôs `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` by default only installs to `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mprefix[0m[1;39m}[0m[35m/[0m[95mbin[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand OSS-Fuzz [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpasses `--[0m[33mprefix[0m[39m=$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, without an explicit `install: true` the binaries are never[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopied under `$OUT`. As a result, `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` in the container is either[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmissing or present without execute permissions, causing bash to return exit status [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m126[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m‚ÄúPermission denied‚Äù[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Targeted File to Patch  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The correct build definitions live in `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`, not the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtop-level `meson.build` that the previous patch wrongly modified [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand which Meson [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrefused to treat as a language file[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. We will leave all root Meson logic and the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer harness untouched.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the two `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` definitions at roughly lines [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m‚Äì[0m[1;36m59[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m61[0m[39m‚Äì[0m[1;36m69[0m[39m:  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m, ‚Ä¶[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m, ‚Ä¶[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. For each target, add:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `install: true`  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      so that Meson will always copy the resulting binary directly under `$OUT` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mthe OSS-Fuzz install prefix[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with the correct execute bits.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. The updated blocks will look like:  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_with: libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        build_by_default: true,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install: true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_with: libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        build_by_default: true,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install: true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Do *not* touch any harness code, Docker mounts, or external files. No changes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto how Meson is invoked in OSS-Fuzz or to the runner script.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ‚Äì Adding `install: true` instructs Meson to include these binaries in its [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstallation step.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ‚Äì Specifying `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ensures they land at the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the OSS-Fuzz `$OUT` directory rather than `$OUT/bin`, matching the runner‚Äôs [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpectation of `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m_mt[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ‚Äì This fixes the ‚ÄúPermission denied‚Äù [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m by both placing the binary [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the right location under the volume bind and preserving executable bits.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ‚Äì All other logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthreading, compile flags, dependencies[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is left intact. We do[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot modify any fuzz harness, avoid messing with cached Meson files, and preserve [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Post-Patch Validation  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reconfigure with Meson and rebuild.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm under the OSS-Fuzz container that `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m` and [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` exist, are executable [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`chmod +x`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and run without [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediate permission errors.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rerun the `run_fuzzer dav1d_fuzzer_mt [0m[33m...[0m[39m` command to verify the exit-status [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m126[0m[39m is resolved.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>tests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:48[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m78[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
